     <script type="text/javascript">
      var postal_code;var reserve_id;var reserve_label;var params=getSearchParameters();if(params.from_reserve=='mobile'&&params.postal_code!=''){if(params.reserve_id!=''&&params.reserve_label!=''){$("#selectedReserve").val(decodeURI(params.reserve_label));$("#reservedid").val(params.reserve_id);setTimeout(function(){reserveDelivery(params.postal_code);},1000);}else{setTimeout(function(){$("#btn-check-reserve-mobile").click();},1000);}}function checkDelivery(postalCode,status){if(typeof postalCode==="undefined"||postalCode==-1){postalCode=$('#check-delivery-postal-mobile').val();}if(postalCode.length!==6){bootbox.alert('Enter a valid 6-digit postal code');}else{dark_cover();var post_url='https://coldstorage.com.sg/checkout/cart/checkdelivery';postal_code=postalCode;$.post(post_url,{postal_code:postalCode},function(data){dark_uncover();obj=data;var monthNames=["Jan","Feb","Mar","Apr","May","Jun","Jul","Aug","Sep","Oct","Nov","Dec"];var weekday=["Sun","Mon","Tue","Wed","Thu","Fri","Sat"];var date=new Date(obj.earliest.date);if(isNaN(date.getDate())){show_notif("Delivery is already packed the next 7 days for this address",'warning');}else{var earliestDay=weekday[date.getDay()];var fulldate=weekday[date.getDay()]+' '+date.getDate()+' '+monthNames[date.getMonth()];var arrDayHeader=Object.keys(obj.timeslot);var timeslot_wrapper_width=arrDayHeader.length*142;var strHtml='';strHtml=strHtml+'<p>Earliest available slot for <strong>'+postalCode+'</strong> is<br /><span class="date">'+fulldate+'</span>, <span class="date">'+obj.earliest.label+'</span></p>';strHtml=strHtml+'<span class="timeslot-nav left"><i class="fa fa-chevron-left"></i></span>'+'<span class="timeslot-nav right"><i class="fa fa-chevron-right"></i></span>'+'<div class="timeslot-wrapper"><div style="width: '+timeslot_wrapper_width+'px;">'+'<div class="day-header">';for(i in arrDayHeader){var date=new Date(arrDayHeader[i]);if(earliestDay==weekday[date.getDay()]){strHtml=strHtml+"<div class='grid-15 selected'><span class='day-title'>"+weekday[date.getDay()]+'</span><br/>'+date.getDate()+' '+monthNames[date.getMonth()]+"</div>";}else{strHtml=strHtml+"<div class='grid-15'><span class='day-title'>"+weekday[date.getDay()]+'</span><br/>'+date.getDate()+' '+monthNames[date.getMonth()]+"</div>";}}strHtml=strHtml+"</div>"+'<div class="clearfix"> </div>';strHtml=strHtml+"<div class='timeslot-content'>";$.each(obj.timeslot,function(day,record){var dateSlot=new Date(day);strHtml=strHtml+"<div class='grid-15'>";keysSorted=Object.keys(record).sort();$.each(keysSorted,function(idx,time){strTimelabel=record[time].label;strTimeslotidx='"'+record[time].timeslot_idx+'"';strTimelabel=strTimelabel.replace(/:00/g,':00');strTimelabel=strTimelabel.replace(/.00/g,':00');strSelectTime='"'+weekday[dateSlot.getDay()]+" "+dateSlot.getDate()+' '+monthNames[date.getMonth()]+", "+strTimelabel+'"';if(record[time].available==true&&status=="yes"){if(params.reserve_id!=undefined&&params.reserve_id.toString()==record[time].timeslot_idx){strHtml=strHtml+"<a class='highlight enable' id='reserved_time' onclick='reserved("+strTimeslotidx+",this,"+strSelectTime+")' >"+strTimelabel+"</a><br/>";}else{strHtml=strHtml+"<a class='highlight enable' onclick='reserved("+strTimeslotidx+",this,"+strSelectTime+")' >"+strTimelabel+"</a><br/>";}}else if(record[time].available==true&&status=="no"){strHtml=strHtml+"<a class='highlight enable' href='javascript:void(0);'>"+strTimelabel+"</a><br/>";}else{strHtml=strHtml+"<a class='highlight disable'>"+strTimelabel+"</a><br/>";}});strHtml=strHtml+"</div>";});strHtml=strHtml+'</div>'+'<div class="clearfix"> </div>'+'</div></div>';selectedReserve=$("#selectedReserve").val();var bootbox_buttons={main:{label:"Login To Reserve",size:'large',className:"btn-primary login-popup",callback:function(){var new_url=replaceUrlParam(window.location.href,'from_reserve','mobile').split('?')[1];window.history.pushState('object','New Title',"?"+new_url);var new_url=replaceUrlParam(window.location.href,'postal_code',postal_code).split('?')[1];window.history.pushState('object','New Title',"?"+new_url);var new_url=replaceUrlParam(window.location.href,'reserve_id',reserve_id).split('?')[1];window.history.pushState('object','New Title',"?"+new_url);var new_url=replaceUrlParam(window.location.href,'reserve_label',reserve_label).split('?')[1];window.history.pushState('object','New Title',"?"+new_url);$(".btn-login-mobile").click();}}};bootbox.dialog({message:strHtml,title:"Select Your Delivery Slot",className:"reserve-delivery-dialog-mobile",buttons:bootbox_buttons,show:false}).off("shown.bs.modal").on("shown.bs.modal",function(){var btn_primary=$(this).find('.modal-footer .btn-primary, .modal-footer .btn-warning');btn_primary.each(function(i,v){var text=$(this).text();$(this).html('<span class="display-static reserve-delivery-button">'+text+'</span>');});}).modal('show');$('#reserved_time').click();$('.reserve-delivery-dialog .modal-footer').append('<p class="register">Don\'t have an account with us yet? <a href="javascript:;" class="signup-popup">Register Now</a></p>');$(".signup-popup").click(function(){bootbox.hideAll()
$(".btn-register-mobile").click();});}},'json');}}function reserveDelivery(postalCode){var post_url=site_config.base_path+'checkout/cart/reserveTimeslot';$.post(post_url,{timeslot:$("#reservedid").val(),postal:postalCode},function(data){obj=JSON.parse(data);if(obj.valid){var notif='You have selected the following delivery slot: <b style="color: #00b050;">'+$("#selectedReserve").val()+'</b>';show_notif(notif);$('.text-reserve').html('Your delivery slot: <b>'+$("#selectedReserve").val()+'</b>').addClass('reserved');localStorage.setItem("reservedslot",$("#selectedReserve").val());$("#selectedReserve").val('');$("#reservedid").val('');reserve_slot.init();if(typeof normal_delivery_slot=='object'&&typeof checkout_cart=='object'){normal_delivery_slot.get_delivery_timeslot(checkout_cart.getActiveAddressPostalCode());}var newUrl=window.location.href.split('?')[0]
window.history.pushState("object or string","Title",newUrl);}else{if(typeof obj.message==="undefined"){show_notif('Failed to reserve.');}else{show_notif(obj.message);}$("#reservedid").val('');}});}function replaceUrlParam(url,paramName,paramValue){if(paramValue==null)paramValue='';url=url.replace('?name=','');var pattern=new RegExp('\\b('+paramName+'=).*?(&|$)')
if(url.search(pattern)>=0){return url.replace(pattern,'$1'+paramValue+'$2');}return url+(url.indexOf('?')>0?'&':'?')+paramName+'='+paramValue}function getSearchParameters(){var prmstr=window.location.search.substr(1);return prmstr!=null&&prmstr!=""?transformToAssocArray(prmstr):{};}function transformToAssocArray(prmstr){var params={};var prmarr=prmstr.split("&");for(var i=0;i<prmarr.length;i++){var tmparr=prmarr[i].split("=");params[tmparr[0]]=tmparr[1];}return params;}function reserved(timeslotIdx,elm,strSelectTime){reserve_id=timeslotIdx;reserve_label=strSelectTime;$("#reservedid").val(timeslotIdx);$("#selectedReserve").val(strSelectTime);$(".reserve-delivery-dialog-mobile .reserved").removeClass("reserved");$(elm).addClass("reserved");}$(function(){if(typeof localStorage.reservedslot!=="undefined"){$('.text-reserve').html('Your delivery slot: <b>'+localStorage.reservedslot+'</b>').addClass('reserved');}$(document).on('click','.timeslot-nav.left',function(){var val=$('.timeslot-wrapper').scrollLeft();val=parseInt(val)-142;$('.timeslot-wrapper').scrollLeft(val);});$(document).on('click','.timeslot-nav.right',function(){var val=$('.timeslot-wrapper').scrollLeft();val=parseInt(val)+142;$('.timeslot-wrapper').scrollLeft(val);});});
     </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var add_shoppinglist_url='https://coldstorage.com.sg/shoppinglist/default/create_shoppinglist';var shopping_list_product_id;var shopping_list_quantity;var option_list=false;function gotoShoppingList(){$(".btn-shopping-list").click();}function openShoppingListDialog(element){$.fancybox.close(true);$(".btn-shopping-list").click();}function addList(element,type){var selIndex=$("#shopping-list-select-id option:selected").val();if(selIndex>=0){addToShoppingList(element,'simple');}else{newSaveShoppinglist(element,'simple');}}function addToShoppingList(element,type,cart_id){bootbox.hideAll();if(cart_id==undefined){var selIndex=$("#shopping-list-select-id option:selected").val();}else{var selIndex=cart_id;}if(selIndex>=0){dark_cover();var qty=0;if(type=='simple'){var qty=shopping_list_quantity;}else if(type=='configurable'){var qty=shopping_list_quantity;}if(qty>0){var post_url='https://coldstorage.com.sg/shoppinglist/default/add_shoppinglist_item';$.post(post_url,{cart_id:selIndex,product_id:shopping_list_product_id,qty:qty},function(data){greyedItem(shopping_list_product_id);dark_uncover();show_topstack_notif('success','<div class="notif">The product has been added to your Wishlist</div><br/>');});}else{dark_uncover();show_topstack_notif('error','<div class="notif">Please enter a valid qty of item to be added to your Wishlist!</div><br/>');}document.getElementById('txtProductID').value="";}else{show_alert_error('Please select your Wishlist first!');}}function newSaveShoppinglist(element,type){bootbox.hideAll();var new_name=$('#newlist').val();if(new_name!=''){$.post(add_shoppinglist_url,{name:new_name,type:"cart_id"},function(data){option_list='<option value="'+data.cart_id+'">'+new_name+'</option>';addToShoppingList(element,'simple',data.cart_id);});}else{show_alert_error('Please enter your Wishlist name!');}}function greyedItem(prod_id){$(".heart.btn-add-to-shopping-list[data-product-id='"+prod_id+"']").parent().addClass('greyed');$(".heart.btn-add-to-shopping-list[data-product-id='"+prod_id+"']").attr('data-original-title','Item Already Added');}$(function(){$('body').on('click','.btn-add-to-shopping-list',function(){shopping_list_product_id=$(this).data('product-id');shopping_list_quantity=$(this).data('qty');if(!$(this).parent().hasClass('greyed')){openShoppingListDialog($(this));}});});
  </script>

                              <script>
                               var brand_list='';var minprice='';var maxprice='';var slider=document.getElementById('price-slider');var slider_mobile=document.getElementById('price-slider-mobile');var lowest=1.2;var highest=146.40;var start=1.2;var end=146.40;var order=7;if($('#price-slider').length>0){noUiSlider.create(slider,{start:[lowest,highest],connect:true,range:{'min':start,'max':end}});noUiSlider.create(slider_mobile,{start:[lowest,highest],connect:true,range:{'min':start,'max':end}});var Values=[document.getElementById('value-lower-desktop'),document.getElementById('value-upper-desktop')];var Values_mobile=[document.getElementById('value-lower-mobile'),document.getElementById('value-upper-mobile')];}if($('#price-slider').length>0){slider.noUiSlider.on('update',function(values,handle){Values[handle].innerHTML=values[handle];});slider_mobile.noUiSlider.on('update',function(values,handle){Values_mobile[handle].innerHTML=values[handle];});slider.noUiSlider.on('set',function(){minprice=$('#value-lower-desktop').html();maxprice=$('#value-upper-desktop').html();if(start==minprice&&end==maxprice){$('.icon_circle.price').hide();}else{$('.icon_circle.price').show();}if(minprice==''){var new_url=removeQueryStringParameter(window.location.href,'minprice');}else{var new_url=replaceUrlParam(window.location.href,'minprice',minprice).split('?')[1];}window.history.pushState('object','New Title',"?"+new_url);if(maxprice==''){var new_url=removeQueryStringParameter(window.location.href,'maxprice');}else{var new_url=replaceUrlParam(window.location.href,'maxprice',maxprice).split('?')[1];}window.history.pushState('object','New Title',"?"+new_url);setTimeout(function(){doAjaxUpdate();},500);});slider_mobile.noUiSlider.on('set',function(){minprice=$('#value-lower-mobile').html();maxprice=$('#value-upper-mobile').html();if(minprice==''){var new_url=removeQueryStringParameter(window.location.href,'minprice');}else{var new_url=replaceUrlParam(window.location.href,'minprice',minprice).split('?')[1];}window.history.pushState('object','New Title',"?"+new_url);if(maxprice==''){var new_url=removeQueryStringParameter(window.location.href,'maxprice');}else{var new_url=replaceUrlParam(window.location.href,'maxprice',maxprice).split('?')[1];}window.history.pushState('object','New Title',"?"+new_url);setTimeout(function(){doAjaxUpdate();},500);});}$(document).ready(function(){$(".button-filter-wrapper").fancybox({maxWidth:400,maxHeight:600,fitToView:true,width:'90%',height:'90%',autoSize:true,closeClick:false,openEffect:'none',closeEffect:'none',tpl:{closeBtn:'<a title="Close" class="fancybox-item fancybox-close myClose" href="javascript:;"></a>'},afterShow:function(){}});});$('.accordion_title a').on('click',function(e){$(this).parent().parent().find('.accordion_content').slideToggle();$(this).parent().find(".title_right i").toggleClass('fa-chevron-circle-down fa-chevron-circle-up');});$(document).on('click','.checkfilter-brand',function(){if(this.checked){var sval=brand_list;if(sval==""){brand_list=this.value+"_";}else{brand_list=sval+this.value+"_";}}else{brand_list=brand_list.replace(this.value+"_","");}if(brand_list==''){$('.icon_circle.brand').hide();var new_url=removeQueryStringParameter(window.location.href,'fbrand');}else{$('.icon_circle.brand').show();var new_url=replaceUrlParam(window.location.href,'fbrand',brand_list).split('?')[1];}window.history.pushState('object','New Title',"?"+new_url);setTimeout(function(){doAjaxUpdate();},500);});$(document).on('click','.checkfilter-attribute',function(){var attribute_param=$(this).attr('data-attribute-parameter');var header_slug=$(this).attr('data-header-slug');var attribute_object=$('.attribute_array[data-attribute-parameter="'+attribute_param+'"]');var attribute_id=attribute_object.attr('data-attribute-id');var temp_value=attribute_object.val();if(this.checked){var sval=temp_value;if(sval==""){temp_value=this.value+"_";}else{temp_value=sval+this.value+"_";}}else{temp_value=temp_value.replace(this.value+"_","");}attribute_object.val(temp_value);if(temp_value==''){$('.icon_circle.'+header_slug).hide();var new_url=removeQueryStringParameter(window.location.href,attribute_param);}else{$('.icon_circle.'+header_slug).show();var new_url=replaceUrlParam(window.location.href,attribute_param,temp_value).split('?')[1];}window.history.pushState('object','New Title',"?"+new_url);setTimeout(function(){doAjaxUpdate();},500);});
